\DoxyCodeLine{02957 \textcolor{comment}{                    //  Permute columns k-\/1 and k of R\_R and Z}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02958 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:63' R\_R(1:i,[i1,i]) = R\_R(1:i,[i,i1]);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02959 \textcolor{comment}{                    sizes[0] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02960 \textcolor{comment}{                    sizes[1] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02961 \textcolor{comment}{                    c\_result[0] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02962 \textcolor{comment}{                    c\_result[1] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02963 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_loop\_ub = static\_cast<int>(c\_i);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02964 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_R.resize(static\_cast<int>(c\_i), 2);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02965 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i1 = 0; i1 < 2; i1++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02966 \textcolor{comment}{                        for (i2 = 0; i2 < b\_loop\_ub; i2++) \{ b\_R[i2 + b\_n * i1] = R\_R[i2 + n * c\_result[i1]]; \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02967 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02968 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_loop\_ub = b\_n;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02969 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i1 = 0; i1 < 2; i1++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02970 \textcolor{comment}{                        for (i2 = 0; i2 < b\_loop\_ub; i2++) \{ R\_R[i2 + n * sizes[i1]] = b\_R[i2 + b\_n * i1]; \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02971 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02972 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:64' Z(:,[i1,i]) = Z(:,[i,i1]);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02973 \textcolor{comment}{                    sizes[0] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02974 \textcolor{comment}{                    sizes[1] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02975 \textcolor{comment}{                    input\_sizes\_idx\_1 = n -\/ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02976 \textcolor{comment}{                    c\_result[0] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02977 \textcolor{comment}{                    c\_result[1] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02978 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_R.resize(n, 2);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02979 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i1 = 0; i1 < 2; i1++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02980 \textcolor{comment}{                        for (i2 = 0; i2 <= input\_sizes\_idx\_1; i2++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02981 \textcolor{comment}{                            b\_R[i2 + b\_n * i1] = Z[i2 + n * c\_result[i1]];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02982 \textcolor{comment}{                        \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02983 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02984 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_loop\_ub = b\_n;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02985 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i1 = 0; i1 < 2; i1++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02986 \textcolor{comment}{                        for (i2 = 0; i2 < b\_loop\_ub; i2++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02987 \textcolor{comment}{                            Z[i2 + n * sizes[i1]] = b\_R[i2 + b\_n * i1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02988 \textcolor{comment}{                        \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02989 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02990 \textcolor{comment}{                \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02991 \textcolor{comment}{            \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02992 \textcolor{comment}{            // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:68' for i = 2:2:n}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02993 \textcolor{comment}{            for (b\_i = 0; b\_i < i; b\_i++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02994 \textcolor{comment}{                c\_i = (b\_i << 1) + 2U;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02995 \textcolor{comment}{                // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:69' i1 = i-\/1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02996 \textcolor{comment}{                // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:70' if swap(i) == 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02997 \textcolor{comment}{                if (vi[static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1] == 1.0) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02998 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:71' [G,R\_R([i1,i],i1)] = planerot(R\_R([i1,i],i1));}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02999 \textcolor{comment}{                    low\_tmp[0] = R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2)) -\/ 2];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03000 \textcolor{comment}{                    low\_tmp[1] = R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2)) -\/ 1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03001 \textcolor{comment}{                    helper::planerot<scalar, index>(low\_tmp, G);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03002 \textcolor{comment}{                    R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2)) -\/ 2] = low\_tmp[0];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03003 \textcolor{comment}{                    R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2)) -\/ 1] = low\_tmp[1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03004 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:72' R\_R([i1,i],i:n) = G * R\_R([i1,i],i:n);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03005 \textcolor{comment}{                    if (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) > static\_cast<int>(n)) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03006 \textcolor{comment}{                        i1 = 0;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03007 \textcolor{comment}{                        i2 = 0;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03008 \textcolor{comment}{                        result = 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03009 \textcolor{comment}{                    \} else \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03010 \textcolor{comment}{                        i1 = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03011 \textcolor{comment}{                        i2 = static\_cast<int>(n);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03012 \textcolor{comment}{                        result = static\_cast<int>(c\_i);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03013 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03014 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_loop\_ub = i2 -\/ i1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03015 \textcolor{comment}{                    b.resize(2, b\_loop\_ub);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03016 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i2 = 0; i2 < b\_loop\_ub; i2++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03017 \textcolor{comment}{                        input\_sizes\_idx\_1 = i1 + i2;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03018 \textcolor{comment}{                        b[2 * i2] = R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * input\_sizes\_idx\_1) -\/ 2];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03019 \textcolor{comment}{                        b[2 * i2 + 1] = R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * input\_sizes\_idx\_1) -\/ 1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03020 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03021 \textcolor{comment}{                    helper::internal::blas::mtimes(G, b, r1);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03022 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_loop\_ub = r1.size(1);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03023 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i1 = 0; i1 < b\_loop\_ub; i1++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03024 \textcolor{comment}{                        input\_sizes\_idx\_1 = (result + i1) -\/ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03025 \textcolor{comment}{                        R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * input\_sizes\_idx\_1) -\/ 2] = r1[2 * i1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03026 \textcolor{comment}{                        R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * input\_sizes\_idx\_1) -\/ 1] = r1[2 * i1 + 1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03027 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03028 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:73' y\_L([i1,i]) = G * y\_L([i1,i]);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03029 \textcolor{comment}{                    low\_tmp[0] = y\_r[static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03030 \textcolor{comment}{                    low\_tmp[1] = y\_r[static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03031 \textcolor{comment}{                    y\_r[static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2] = G[0] * low\_tmp[0] + low\_tmp[1] * G[2];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03032 \textcolor{comment}{                    y\_r[static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1] = low\_tmp[0] * G[1] + low\_tmp[1] * G[3];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03033 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:74' swap(i) = 0;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03034 \textcolor{comment}{                    vi[static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1] = 0.0;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03035 \textcolor{comment}{                \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03036 \textcolor{comment}{            \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03037 \textcolor{comment}{            // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:77' for i = 3:2:n}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03038 \textcolor{comment}{            i = static\_cast<int>((n + -\/1.0) / 2.0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03039 \textcolor{comment}{            for (b\_i = 0; b\_i < i; b\_i++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03040 \textcolor{comment}{                c\_i = static\_cast<unsigned int>((b\_i << 1) + 3);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03041 \textcolor{comment}{                // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:78' i1 = i-\/1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03042 \textcolor{comment}{                // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:79' zeta = round(R\_R(i1,i) / R\_R(i1,i1));}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03043 \textcolor{comment}{                zeta = std::round(R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1)) -\/ 2] /}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03044 \textcolor{comment}{                                  R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2)) -\/ 2]);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03045 \textcolor{comment}{                // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:80' alpha = R\_R(i1,i) -\/ zeta * R\_R(i1,i1);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03046 \textcolor{comment}{                input\_sizes\_idx\_1 = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03047 \textcolor{comment}{                s = R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2)) -\/ 2];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03048 \textcolor{comment}{                alpha = R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1)) -\/ 2] -\/ zeta * s;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03049 \textcolor{comment}{                // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:81' if R\_R(i1,i1)\string^2 > (1 + 1.e-\/0) * (alpha\string^2 +}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03050 \textcolor{comment}{                // R\_R(i,i)\string^2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03051 \textcolor{comment}{                a = R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1)) -\/ 1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03052 \textcolor{comment}{                if ((s * s > 2.0 * (alpha * alpha + a * a)) \&\& (zeta != 0.0)) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03053 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:82' if zeta \string~= 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03054 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:83' f = true;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03055 \textcolor{comment}{                    f = true;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03056 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:84' swap(i) = 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03057 \textcolor{comment}{                    vi[static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1] = 1.0;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03058 \textcolor{comment}{                    //  Perform a size reduction on R\_R(k-\/1,k)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03059 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:86' R\_R(i1,i) = alpha;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03060 \textcolor{comment}{                    R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1)) -\/ 2] = alpha;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03061 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:87' R\_R(1:i-\/2,i) = R\_R(1:i-\/2,i) -\/ zeta * R\_R(1:i-\/2,i-\/1);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03062 \textcolor{comment}{                    vr.resize(input\_sizes\_idx\_1);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03063 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i1 = 0; i1 < input\_sizes\_idx\_1; i1++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03064 \textcolor{comment}{                        vr[i1] = R\_R[i1 + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1)] -\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03065 \textcolor{comment}{                                 zeta * R\_R[i1 + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2)];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03066 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03067 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_loop\_ub = vn;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03068 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i1 = 0; i1 < b\_loop\_ub; i1++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03069 \textcolor{comment}{                        R\_R[i1 + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1)] = vr[i1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03070 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03071 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:88' Z(:,i) = Z(:,i) -\/ zeta * Z(:,i-\/1);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03072 \textcolor{comment}{                    input\_sizes\_idx\_1 = n -\/ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03073 \textcolor{comment}{                    vr.resize(n);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03074 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i1 = 0; i1 <= input\_sizes\_idx\_1; i1++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03075 \textcolor{comment}{                        vr[i1] = Z[i1 + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1)] -\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03076 \textcolor{comment}{                                 zeta * Z[i1 + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2)];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03077 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03078 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_loop\_ub = vn;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03079 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i1 = 0; i1 < b\_loop\_ub; i1++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03080 \textcolor{comment}{                        Z[i1 + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1)] = vr[i1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03081 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03082 \textcolor{comment}{                    //  Permute columns k-\/1 and k of R\_R and Z}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03083 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:91' R\_R(1:i,[i1,i]) = R\_R(1:i,[i,i1]);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03084 \textcolor{comment}{                    sizes[0] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03085 \textcolor{comment}{                    sizes[1] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03086 \textcolor{comment}{                    c\_result[0] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03087 \textcolor{comment}{                    c\_result[1] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03088 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_loop\_ub = static\_cast<int>(c\_i);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03089 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_R.resize(static\_cast<int>(c\_i), 2);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03090 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i1 = 0; i1 < 2; i1++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03091 \textcolor{comment}{                        for (i2 = 0; i2 < b\_loop\_ub; i2++) \{ b\_R[i2 + b\_n * i1] = R\_R[i2 + n * c\_result[i1]]; \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03092 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03093 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_loop\_ub = b\_n;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03094 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i1 = 0; i1 < 2; i1++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03095 \textcolor{comment}{                        for (i2 = 0; i2 < b\_loop\_ub; i2++) \{ R\_R[i2 + n * sizes[i1]] = b\_R[i2 + b\_n * i1]; \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03096 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03097 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:92' Z(:,[i1,i]) = Z(:,[i,i1]);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03098 \textcolor{comment}{                    sizes[0] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03099 \textcolor{comment}{                    sizes[1] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03100 \textcolor{comment}{                    input\_sizes\_idx\_1 = n -\/ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03101 \textcolor{comment}{                    c\_result[0] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03102 \textcolor{comment}{                    c\_result[1] = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03103 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_R.resize(n, 2);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03104 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i1 = 0; i1 < 2; i1++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03105 \textcolor{comment}{                        for (i2 = 0; i2 <= input\_sizes\_idx\_1; i2++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03106 \textcolor{comment}{                            b\_R[i2 + b\_n * i1] = Z[i2 + n * c\_result[i1]];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03107 \textcolor{comment}{                        \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03108 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03109 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_loop\_ub = b\_n;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03110 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i1 = 0; i1 < 2; i1++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03111 \textcolor{comment}{                        for (i2 = 0; i2 < b\_loop\_ub; i2++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03112 \textcolor{comment}{                            Z[i2 + n * sizes[i1]] = b\_R[i2 + b\_n * i1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03113 \textcolor{comment}{                        \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03114 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03115 \textcolor{comment}{                \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03116 \textcolor{comment}{            \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03117 \textcolor{comment}{            // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:96' for i = 3:2:n}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03118 \textcolor{comment}{            for (b\_i = 0; b\_i < i; b\_i++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03119 \textcolor{comment}{                c\_i = static\_cast<unsigned int>((b\_i << 1) + 3);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03120 \textcolor{comment}{                // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:97' i1 = i-\/1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03121 \textcolor{comment}{                // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:98' if swap(i) == 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03122 \textcolor{comment}{                if (vi[static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1] == 1.0) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03123 \textcolor{comment}{                    //  Bring R\_R baci to an upper triangular matrix by a Givens rotation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03124 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:100' [G,R\_R([i1,i],i1)] = planerot(R\_R([i1,i],i1));}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03125 \textcolor{comment}{                    low\_tmp[0] = R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2)) -\/ 2];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03126 \textcolor{comment}{                    low\_tmp[1] = R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2)) -\/ 1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03127 \textcolor{comment}{                    helper::planerot<scalar, index>(low\_tmp, G);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03128 \textcolor{comment}{                    R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2)) -\/ 2] = low\_tmp[0];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03129 \textcolor{comment}{                    R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2)) -\/ 1] = low\_tmp[1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03130 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:101' R\_R([i1,i],i:n) = G * R\_R([i1,i],i:n);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03131 \textcolor{comment}{                    if (static\_cast<int>(c\_i) > static\_cast<int>(n)) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03132 \textcolor{comment}{                        i1 = 0;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03133 \textcolor{comment}{                        i2 = 0;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03134 \textcolor{comment}{                        result = 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03135 \textcolor{comment}{                    \} else \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03136 \textcolor{comment}{                        i1 = static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03137 \textcolor{comment}{                        i2 = static\_cast<int>(n);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03138 \textcolor{comment}{                        result = static\_cast<int>(c\_i);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03139 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03140 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_loop\_ub = i2 -\/ i1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03141 \textcolor{comment}{                    b.resize(2, b\_loop\_ub);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03142 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i2 = 0; i2 < b\_loop\_ub; i2++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03143 \textcolor{comment}{                        input\_sizes\_idx\_1 = i1 + i2;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03144 \textcolor{comment}{                        b[2 * i2] = R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * input\_sizes\_idx\_1) -\/ 2];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03145 \textcolor{comment}{                        b[2 * i2 + 1] = R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * input\_sizes\_idx\_1) -\/ 1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03146 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03147 \textcolor{comment}{                    helper::internal::blas::mtimes(G, b, r1);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03148 \textcolor{comment}{                    b\_loop\_ub = r1.size(1);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03149 \textcolor{comment}{                    for (i1 = 0; i1 < b\_loop\_ub; i1++) \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03150 \textcolor{comment}{                        input\_sizes\_idx\_1 = (result + i1) -\/ 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03151 \textcolor{comment}{                        R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * input\_sizes\_idx\_1) -\/ 2] = r1[2 * i1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03152 \textcolor{comment}{                        R\_R[(static\_cast<int>(c\_i) + n * input\_sizes\_idx\_1) -\/ 1] = r1[2 * i1 + 1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03153 \textcolor{comment}{                    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03154 \textcolor{comment}{                    //  Apply the Givens rotation to y\_r}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03155 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:104' y\_r([i1,i]) = G * y\_r([i1,i]);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03156 \textcolor{comment}{                    low\_tmp[0] = y\_r[static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03157 \textcolor{comment}{                    low\_tmp[1] = y\_r[static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03158 \textcolor{comment}{                    y\_r[static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 2] = G[0] * low\_tmp[0] + low\_tmp[1] * G[2];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03159 \textcolor{comment}{                    y\_r[static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1] = low\_tmp[0] * G[1] + low\_tmp[1] * G[3];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03160 \textcolor{comment}{                    // 'eo\_sils\_reduction:105' swap(i) = 0;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03161 \textcolor{comment}{                    vi[static\_cast<int>(c\_i) -\/ 1] = 0.0;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03162 \textcolor{comment}{                \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03163 \textcolor{comment}{            \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03164 \textcolor{comment}{        \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03165 \textcolor{comment}{        time = omp\_get\_wtime() -\/ time;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03166 \textcolor{comment}{        return time;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03167 \textcolor{comment}{    \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03168 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\end{DoxyCode}
